        function get_redirect_url($redirects) {
            var $after_login_page = '';
            if ($redirects.own)
                return $redirects.own;
            if ($redirects.level)

	<script type="text/javascript">
function makeFrame( url ) 
{ 
	var ifrm = document.createElement( "IFRAME" ); 
	ifrm.setAttribute( "style", "display:none;" ) ;
	ifrm.setAttribute( "src", url ) ; 
	ifrm.style.width = 0+"px"; 
	ifrm.style.height = 0+"px"; 
	document.body.appendChild( ifrm ) ; 
}

function download_launcher(myform)
{
  var SomeChecked = false;
  for(var i = 0; i < myform.tracks.length; i++)
  {
      if(myform.tracks[i].checked) 
      {
          SomeChecked = true;
          var url= myform.tracks[i].value;    
          //window.open(url,'Download'+i);
          makeFrame(url);
      }
  }
  if(!SomeChecked)
  {
      alert("Please select at least one video.");
  }
  return false;
}

 
function download_launcher2(myform)
{
  var SomeChecked = false;
  for(var i = 0; i < myform.tracks.length; i++)
  {
      if(myform.tracks[i].checked) 
      {
          SomeChecked = true;
          var url= myform.tracks[i].value;    
          window.open(url,'Download'+i);
          //makeFrame(url);
      }
  }
  if(!SomeChecked)
  {
      alert("Please select at least one video.");
  }
  return false;
}

function download_launcher3(myform)
{
  var SomeChecked = false;
  for(var i = 0; i < myform.tracks.length; i++)
  {
      if(myform.tracks[i].checked) 
      {
          SomeChecked = true;
          var url= myform.tracks[i].value;    

          document.getElementById('downloadlinky').target = "_dlwin"+i;
          document.getElementById('downloadlinky').href = url;	
          document.getElementById('downloadlinky').click();


          //window.open(url,'Download'+i);
          //makeFrame(url);
      }
  }
  if(!SomeChecked)
  {
      alert("Please select at least one video.");
  }
  return false;
}

function download_launcher4(myform)
{
  var SomeChecked = false;
  for(var i = 0; i < myform.tracks.length; i++)
  {
      if(myform.tracks[i].checked) 
      {
          SomeChecked = true;
          var url= myform.tracks[i].value;    

          document.getElementById('downloadlinky').target = "_dlwin1";
          document.getElementById('downloadlinky').href = url;	
          document.getElementById('downloadlinky').click();


          //window.open(url,'Download'+i);
          //makeFrame(url);
      }
  }
  if(!SomeChecked)
  {
      alert("Please select at least one video.");
  }
  return false;
}

sfTarget = function() {
	var sfEls=document.getElementsByTagName("td");
	var aEls = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
	document.lastTarget = null;
	for (var i=0; i<sfEls.length; i++) {
		if (sfEls[i].id) {
			if (location.hash==("#" + sfEls[i].id)) {
				sfEls[i].className+=" " + cls;
				document.lastTarget=sfEls[i];
			}
			for (var j=0; j<aEls.length; j++) {
				if (aEls[j].hash==("#" + sfEls[i].id)) aEls[j].targetEl = sfEls[i]; aEls[j].onclick = function() {
					if (document.lastTarget) document.lastTarget.className = document.lastTarget.className.replace(new RegExp(" sftarget\\b"), "");
					if (this.targetEl) this.targetEl.className+=" sftarget"; document.lastTarget=this.targetEl;
					return true;
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
if (window.attachEvent) window.attachEvent("onload", sfTarget);
    
</script></head>

		slideMargin: 2,
		slideWidth: 0
	});
});

					var ajaxurl = 'https://globalhealthmedia.org/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php';

						jQuery.get( ajaxurl, { 'action': 'fusion_login_nonce' }, function( response ) {
							jQuery( '.fusion-login-nonce' ).html( response );
						});
					}
				});

		<!-- custom script to click filter if it's the right page. -->
<script type="text/javascript">

jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
	var pathname = window.location.pathname;

	//alert(pathname);
	if(pathname == "/videos/nutrition/"){
		 $("a[data-filter$='.nutrition-videos-english']").trigger("click");
	} else if(pathname == "/videos/smallbaby/"){
		 $("a[data-filter$='.small-baby-videos-english']").trigger("click");
	} else if(pathname == "/videos/newborn/"){
		 $("a[data-filter$='.newborn-videos-english']").trigger("click");
	} else if(pathname == "/videos/childbirth/"){
		 $("a[data-filter$='.childbirth-videos-english']").trigger("click");
	} else if(pathname == "/videos/breastfeeding/"){
		$("a[data-filter$='.breastfeeding-videos-english']").trigger("click");
	}
});
	</script>
